class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1">30W charging speed in a USB-C battery isn’t all that impressive, except when it comes in a compact package. Anker’s 10,000mAh power bank seems like a great fit for anyone who needs to quickly fill up their phone or tablet without sacrificing bag space. And now, it’s cheaper than ever at <a rel="sponsored" href="https://www.amazon.com/Anker-Portable-Charger-Charging-Battery/dp/B0CZ9M6X8Q/?th=1&amp;tag=theverge02-20">Amazon</a>, where you can snag one for $12.94 in one of four colors.</p></div><div class="wn1wvof"><p class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1">This battery’s other big selling point is that it has a built-in USB-C charging cable that doubles as a handle, so no need to bring your own (and no worries if you forget one).</p></div><div class="_1t4tcr94">Devastating wildfires in Canada are creating an air quality disaster in the US.</div><div class="wn1wvof wn1wvo0"><p class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1">The worst <a href="https://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/saskatchewan/is-climate-change-the-cause-of-saskatchewans-wildfire-1.7548474">wildfires in decades</a> are tearing through Saskatchewan, Canada, and at least <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2025/05/15/world/canada/canada-wildfires-manitoba-deaths.html">two people</a> have been killed in blazes in the neighboring province of Manitoba.</p></div><div class="wn1wvof"><p class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1"><a href="https://www.nytimes.com/article/canada-wildfires-2025.html">Smoke from those fires has triggered air quality warnings</a> in Michigan, Wisconsin, and Minnesota. It’s the kind of climate change-driven disaster that led young people from Minnesota to <a href="/news/677537/youth-climate-change-lawsuit-trump-executive-orders">file suit against the Trump administration</a> last week. Wildfire smoke can be <a href="https://news.stanford.edu/stories/2025/01/assessing-wildfire-health-risks">10 times as toxic</a> as other air pollutants.</p></div></div><div><div class="wn1wvoc"><div class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1">The first is <a href="https://tax.thomsonreuters.com/en/accounting-solutions/c/cocounsel-tax/cocounsel-ai-for-tax-audit-and-accounting-professionals">CoCounsel for tax, audit, and accounting professionals</a>, which option to set Perplexity as their default assistant instead of Google Gemini.</p></div></div><div><div class="wn1wvoe"><div class="wn1wvo9"><a class="wn1wvoa" class="_1t4tcr94">Tango Gameworks relaunches with a new look.</div><div class="wn1wvof wn1wvo0"><p class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1">After the former Microsoft game studio behind <em>Hi-Fi Rush</em> was <a href="/2024/8/12/24218424/hifi-rush-studio-tango-gameworks-saved-krafton-microsoft">spared from closure last year</a>, Tango Gameworks now has a <a href="https://tangogameworks.com/2025/06/02/tango-gameworks-relaunch-with-new-website/">new website and updated branding</a>. The studio is hiring for multiple positions and says its redesigned look and logo represent its vision as a “creative workshop” for creating games that feel “handmade with soul.”</p></div></div><div><div class="wn1wvoc"><div style="position:relative"><div class="_1ymtmqpj"><div class=""><div style="background-image:none" class="duet--media--content-warning ucljxw0"><div 22.4796Z"></path></svg></button></div></div><div class="_1t4tcr90"><div class="_1t4tcr94">iPhone users can finally copy chunks of WhatsApp messages.</div><div class="wn1wvof wn1wvo0"><p class="duet--article--dangerously-set-cms-markup duet--article--standard-paragraph _1ymtmqpi _17nnmdy1 _17nnmdy0 _1xwtict1">The <a href="https://wabetainfo.com/whatsapp-for-ios-25-16-81-whats-new/">WhatsApp for iOS 25.16.81 update</a> that’s rolling out over the coming weeks allows users to hold down on a message to select and copy specific sections, instead of being forced to copy <a href="https://faq.whatsapp.com/343365925097133/?cms_platform=iphone&amp;helpref=platform_switcher">the entire message text</a>. Android users are still stuck with this limitation for now, but <em>WABetaInfo</em> reports that a <a href="https://wabetainfo.com/whatsapp-beta-for-android-2-25-18-3-whats-new/">similar update is in the works</a>.</p></div></div><div><div class="wn1wvoc"><div style="position:relative"><div class="_1ymtmqpj"><div class=""><div style="background-image:none" class="duet--media--content-warning
